***назреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a> (24990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назревать.html>назрева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen, to become ripe, to mature, (abscess) to come to a head</li>
<li>to be about to happen, to boil up, to be brewing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">voprós <b>nazrél</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the question is ripe; the question cannot be put off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кризис.html>кри́зис</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krízis <b>nazrél</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">things have reached a crisis point; crisis is brewing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:называвший.html>называ́вший</a> (360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:называвший.html>называ́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazyvávšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:называть.html>называ́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nazyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:называться.html>называ́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazyvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назваться.html>назва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to identify oneself, to give one’s name</li>
<li>to be called, to be named</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:называть.html>называ́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nazyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зы<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:назваться.html>назва́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-зыв-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

***наибольший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наибольший.html>наибо́льший</a> (6274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наибольший.html>наибо́льший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naibólʹšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">superlative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹšój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>:
<ol><li>the greatest, the largest, the most</li>
<li>the worst <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in negative context</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>maximal, maximum</li></ol></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ива.html>и́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***наигрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наигрывать.html>наи́грывать</a> (25738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наигра́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naigrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наигрывать.html>наи́грывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naígryvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наигра́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (several songs, pieces or theatrical roles)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gain (some money) gambling or playing a musical instrument</li>
<li>to play <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">quietly or only the main melody, on a musical instrument</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to play (a song or piece) for a recording</li>
<li>to record the music of (a record or film)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тие</a> (25683)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naitie</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; constructed as if <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naítije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тий</a></b>)

***найти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a> (211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*najьti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">find</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically derivable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to find
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Вся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a></i></span>”, performed by t.A.T.u:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найдёшь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нелюбимый.html>нелюби́мых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома́х</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарваться.html>нарвёшься</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́нах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:впотьмах.html>впотьма́х</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i sebjá ne <b>najdjóšʹ</b> v neljubímyx domáx<br />i narvjóšʹsja na strax kak na mínax vpotʹmáx</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And you will not find yourself in a unloved home<br />And you will run into fear like into mines in the dark</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think, to consider</li>
<li>to come across</li>
<li>to be located, to be situated</li>
<li>to happen to have</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b>най<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,   <a href = vnd.unilang:изолированный.html>изоли́рованное</a> спряжение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ^b/b(9).     <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существовать.html>существу́ет</a> устар. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> деепричастия <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> <i>наше́д</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:употреблявшийся.html>употребля́вшаяся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:преимущественно.html>преиму́щественно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> XIX <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>ве́ке</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:основной.html>Основна́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> прич. страд. — <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>на́йденный</a>: <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найдённый</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-най-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>най<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́сь</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ^b/b(9).      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>находи́ться</a>.

***наказание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ние</a> (2944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказать.html>наказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakazánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>punishment</li>
<li>penalty, chastisement

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>

Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказывавший.html>нака́зывавший</a> (7230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказывавший.html>нака́зывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakázyvavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказывать.html>нака́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
